\doxysubsection*{Additional Inherited Members}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$class U$>$\newline
class A\+M\+M\+::\+D\+D\+S\+Manager$<$ U $>$}

Wrapper interface for managing \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_a_m_m}{A\+MM}} Data Types.

Specialization A~\newline
 This is the specialization template for handling the function pointer type of a class instance for subscribed events.

\index{AMM::DDSManager$<$ U $>$@{AMM::DDSManager$<$ U $>$}!Shutdown@{Shutdown}}
\index{Shutdown@{Shutdown}!AMM::DDSManager$<$ U $>$@{AMM::DDSManager$<$ U $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Shutdown()}{Shutdown()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class U $>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_m_m_1_1_d_d_s_manager}{A\+M\+M\+::\+D\+D\+S\+Manager}}$<$ U $>$\+::Shutdown (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Default shutdown command for the module. Should always be used before exiting the executable, because this ensures all Participant activity is properly terminated and cleaned up for memory management sake on the D\+DS network. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Shutdown routine will not stop if an error flag is raised. Will ignore and continue on. 
\end{DoxyNote}
